 Chandrapur district was earlier known as chanda
according to the 2011 census, the population of 22,04,307 in 36 districts of Maharashtra, Chandrapur is considered to be very important in political terms and on the basis of tradition, this city was earlier known as Chanda
 
 is sthaan kaa pracheen naam lokpur bhi tha, jo aage chalakar indupur or uske baad chandrapur ho gaya
 In the British colonial period it was known as Chanda district and around 1964 the city became Chandrapur
 pracheen kaal main kshetra ke anya sthanon main vairangarh, kosal, bhadravati or markanda shaamil the
 Hindu and Buddhist kings are believed to have ruled the region for a long time
 baad main gondon ne 9veen shatabdi se 1751 tak kshetra par shashan kiya, jiske baad maratha kaal shuru hua
 Raghuji Bhonsle, the last king of the dynasty, died in 1853 and Nagpur province, together with Chandrapur, was declared for the British Empire
 1854 se 1947 main aazaadee milane tak yah british madhya praant kaa hissaa tha
 Chandrapur is a city situated on the banks of the Irai and the waterfall, a tributary of the Wardha River in eastern Maharashtra
 jangal or baaghon ke liye pahachaane jane vaala yah shahar gondkaalin pracheen aitihaasik dharoharon ke liye bhi janaa jaataa he
 There is also a 550 year old fort built by the Gond kings along with the Mahakali Devi, Anchaleshwar Temple
 gatchiroli, nagpur, yavatmal jaise jilon kii seemaa chandrapur se lagati he

 Sanjeev Tyagi and lawyer Gautam Khaitan, along with former Air Force Chief SP Tyagi, have been sent by Delhi's Patiala House Court on CBI remand till December 14 for alleged bribery in the Rs 3600-crore Agusta helicopter deal during the UPA regime
 12 viviipi helicopteron kii kharid main 450 karod rupee kii ghoosekhori se jude is maamle main espi tyaagi ke rishtedaar sanjeev tyaagi or vakil gautam khetaan kii bhi giraftaar hui he
 SP Tyagi retired in 2007, accusing Tyagi and his relatives
 espi tyaagi, sanjeev tyaagi or chandigarh main rahane vaale vakil gautam khetaan ko sibiai mukhyalay main shuukravaar ko poochtacha ke liye bulaayaa gaya tha
 He was arrested after nearly four hours of questioning
 kareeb teen saal pehle saamne aae is maamle main sibiai kii ore se kii gai ye pehali giraftaar he
 The CBI had filed an FIR in 2013 to investigate the allegations of bribery
 ghotaale kaa italy conectionis ghotaale se judi vistrut suchanaaen italy main saarvajanik huin, jahaan sarkari vakeelon ne agasta kii mukhya company finameckainika ke chif ke khilaaf bhrashtachar ke aarope lagaae the
 On April 7 this year, an Italian court convicted two of Finmeccanica's officials for bribing the deal
 jaane tyaagi par kya hai aarope--tatkaaleen airforce chif espi tyaagi par aarope he ki viviipi helicopteron kii oparational kshamta kii maanak oonchai 6 hajaar meter se ghataakar 4500 meter karne ke liye raji hue

 -tyaagi apane upar lage aaropon ko khaarij karte rahe hai
 - SP Tyagi says that the change in standards was a joint decision, involving the Air Force, SPG and other departments
 -jaanch ke daayre main videshi root se paise ke len-dein kaa maamla bhi he
 - CBI alleges that lawyer Khaitan confessed that he took money from Europe's middlemen Guido Hasch and Carlo Gerosa
 haalanki, khetaan ne yah bhi kaha ki ye paise deal ko prabhavit karne ke liye ghoose ke taur par nahin liye gaye
 According to CBI sources, the bribe money reached Tyagi through middlemen and relatives
 1 janvari 2014 ko bharat ne yah deal cancel kar di thi
 The reason was stated to be bribery and violation of the terms of the deal
 -sibiai ne is maamle main tyaagi or 18 anya logon ke khilaaf maamla darj kiya
 These include Tyagi's relatives, middlemen and companies
 -ghoose kaa paisa bharat laane ke liye videshi root kaa istemaal kiya gaya
 The CBI has sent judicial requests to eight countries including Italy, Britain, British Virgin Islands, Tunisia, Singapore to find out how the bribe money reached India from abroad
